\doxysubsection*{Modules}
\begin{DoxyCompactItemize}
\item 
\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_m_s_i_s___core_debug}{Core Debug Registers (\+Core\+Debug)}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Cortex-\/\+M0 Core Debug Registers (D\+CB registers, S\+H\+C\+SR, and D\+F\+SR) are only accessible over D\+AP and not via processor. Therefore they are not covered by the Cortex-\/\+M0 header file. \end{DoxyCompactList}\end{DoxyCompactItemize}
